 2486 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      1 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | *-------------------------------------------------
 2487 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      2 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | * Create_Sprite — Compiled sprite engine
 2488 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      3 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | * Ported from FTA's CREATE.SPRITE.S (1989)
 2489 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      4 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | *
 2490 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
 2491 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
 2492 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | *
 2493 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
 2494 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
 2495 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | *
 2496 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/10CC               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):

 3075 |  3  Checkerboard.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/1438               | * alternating scanlines creates the full checkerboard effect.
